 Many common and bright students studying in our country have a pressing desire to go abroad
 kai log iske liye vishesh taiyaariyaan karte hai
 In such a situation, we are telling you that developed countries like England, Canada, Australia and America have fixed their eligibility to pass the examinations like IELTS for the candidates who want to work and study here
 ab bharat main padhai kar rahe aam va kai baar khaas students ko bhi pataa nahin hota ki IELTS kii bhalaa kya he? aise main jaane IELTS ke bare main
 
 
 What is IELTS? IELTS (international English Language Testing System) is the name of an examination in which the English knowledge test of the candidates working and studying in English speaking countries is taken
 koun letaa he IELTS test?ielts pariksha kaa saajha aayojan University Of Cambridge ESOL Examinations (cambridge ESOL), British Council or IDP karte hai
 It is considered the highest standard of English language in the world
 IELTS ko kahaan he manyata?ielts ko australia, america, canada, newjiland va england jaise deshon kii uniwarsity va rojgaar dene vaali sansthaaen manyata detii hai
 Apart from this, all government institutions and non-resident institutions also recognize this
 kahaan di ja sakati hai IELTS kii pariksha?aaj duniya bhar main IELTS ke 1100 se zyada pariksha centre hai
 Most of these are run by several universities and linguistic schools, including the British Council, IELTS Australia
 vishesh jaankaree ke liye www
 ielts
 org par jaaen
 Test format - It consists of 4 sub-tests, or modules
 padhanaa, likhnaa, sunanaa or bolnaa
 It is mandatory for students to sit for all the exams
 saare students ko ek hi sunne va bolne vaale test main baithna padataa he, jabaki unhen padhane va likhane ke liye alag-alag test dene padate hai
 It depends on the academic or general training module they choose
 pariksha ke maukey par chaaron sab-section va unke liye tay samay-sunanaa - 4 section - 40 item - 30 mintesaamaanya training padhanaa- 3 section - 40 item - 60 mintacdmic padhai- 3 section - 40 item - 60 mintesaamaanya training likhaai- 2 task (150 se 250 shabd) 60 mintacdmic likhaai- 2 task (150 se 250 shabd) 60 minutebolnaa- 11 se 14 minatekul samay 2 ghante 45 minuteiaisthsh Listening test -yah test aadhe ghante tak chalata he
 It consists of 4 sections, which are run on cassette tape
 yah monolog or dialog donon hota he
 It runs only once and all questions have to be answered while listening
 haalanki jawaab dekhne ke libetirikt samaydiya jaataa he
 IELTS Reading test - This test lasts for 1 hour
 ummidavaaron ko acadmic reeding test yaa saamaanya training reeding test diya jaataa he
 The test consists of three sections
 isamen difiklti kaa level badhate kram main hota he
 IELTS Writing Test - This test also lasts for 1 hour
 isamen bhi ummidavaaron ko acadmic yaa saamaanya training modul se hokar guzarana padataa he
 In this, students have to write in two different styles
 isamen koi chwis kii suvidha nahin he
 IELTS Speaking test - It consists of a single interview candidate
 is saakshaatkaar ko record bhi kiya jaataa he
 It occurs in three parts
 khud kaa parichay or saakshaatkaar -isamen candidet ko kisi bhi tay topic par 1 se 2 minute bolnaa hoga
 Then a two-way conversation or dialogue
 yah saakshaatkaar 10 se 15 minute tak chalata he

 Divine Rama Ekadashi of Kartik month

 Learn the best method of worshiping Rambha Ekadashi and its importance
 
 
 kya he ekadshi vrath kaa mahatv
 
 
 The most important and auspicious fruitful fast in the world is Ekadashi fast
 yah har maah main do baar aati he - shukla paksh main or krishna paksh main
 Depending on the conditions of the moon, keep this fast, so that there is no mental problem
 in dinon main vrath rakhane se man or sharir donon swasth rahata he or saamaanya bimaariyaan pareshaan nahin karatin
 This fast is perfect for increasing concentration of mind and for solving problems related to mind
 duniya main aap koi vrath-upwas na bhi rakhen, par agar niyamit rup se ekadshi kaa upwas rakhte hai, to har prakaar kii safalataa aapako mil sakati he
 But fasting of Ekadashi is beneficial only by keeping the rules
 rambha ekadshi vrath kii mahima
 
 
 Rambha Ekadashi i
e
 Rama Ekadashi is the Ekadashi of Kartik Krishna Paksha
 yah chaturmaas kii antim ekadshi he
 Fasting of this Ekadashi not only eliminates sins, but also gives women the gift of a happy married life
 is vrath ke prabhaav se vyakti ko ishwar kii krupa kaa bhi anubhav bhi hota he
 This time Rambha Ekadashi is on 15 October
 kaise rakhen rambha ekadshi kaa vrath, kaise karen puja
 
 
 - Worship Lord Krishna or Keshava in the morning or evening
 - mastak par safed chandan yaa gopi chandan lagaakar pujan karen
 - Offer Panchamrit, flowers and Ritu fruits to Shri Keshav
 - shri krishna ke mantron kaa jaap karen- saath hi gita kaa paath bhi avashya karen- raatri ko chandroday ho jane par dipadaan karen- raatri jaagran karke agar upasna karen to zyada shubh hoga- agle din praatavkaal juute, chaate or vastra kaa daan karen
 - Then finish the fast by drinking lemonade, what are the things to keep in mind on the day of Ekadashi
 
 
 - agar vrath na rakh saken to bhi satvik or halkaa aahaar len
 - Please worship Shri Keshav and recite the Gita
 - vaani or vyavhaar par niyantran rakhen
 - Avoid meat liqueur and intoxicants
